Sounds easy, right?\r\n\r\nThe style of the puzzles in Pepe Porcupine originates from a Japanese game called Sokoban. Sokoban means warehouse keeper in Japanese ((倉庫番 sōkoban).  Sokoban is a type of transport puzzle, in which the player pushes boxes or crates around in a warehouse, trying to get them to storage locations.
